      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/13114292-the-last-hope">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4552039-anna?shelf=warriors">warriors</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1188182462" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17260105694399566554">The Dark Forest is rising, and its power is stronger than ever. Even StarClan is helpless and cannot see the lands by the lake anymore, and the darkness frightens them. The Clans don’t trust each other, and even medicine cats are divided. To battle the forces of the Dark Forest, the Three must find the Fourth… their last hope.<br/><br/>The prophecy speaks of the four cats, but I’ve always thought of them as five, because Ivypool did as much as the Three to win this battle. <b>Ivypool</b> is the one who makes the</span>
  <span id="freeText17260105694399566554" style="display:none">The Dark Forest is rising, and its power is stronger than ever. Even StarClan is helpless and cannot see the lands by the lake anymore, and the darkness frightens them. The Clans don’t trust each other, and even medicine cats are divided. To battle the forces of the Dark Forest, the Three must find the Fourth… their last hope.<br /><br />The prophecy speaks of the four cats, but I’ve always thought of them as five, because Ivypool did as much as the Three to win this battle. <b>Ivypool</b> is the one who makes the biggest sacrifices, though no one knows of them, since her Clanmates don’t know of her struggle and cats she trains with in the Dark Forest think her to be cruel and evil. She had to persuade the Dark Forest in her loyalty, and in doing so, she goes so far that it scares even the living Dark Forest warriors. But in truth, Ivypool does everything not only to protect her Clanmates from the Dark Forest, but also to protect living Dark Forest cats that were tricked into training both from the Dark Forest leaders and from their own Clanmates.<br /><br /><b>Jayfeather</b> is in his usual grumpy and snarky mood for most of the book, but strange thing – instead of being annoying, he was mature and wise. But when StarClan is blind, Clans are at each other throats and even medicine cats don’t trust each other, you need someone like Jayfeather to shake some sense into the heads of the cats gone mad with fear. Jayfeather was born blind, but in some aspects he can see better than sighted – and in the end Jayfeather does something that only he could possibly do. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He actually gathers all of StarClan, tells them how stupid they were by ignoring the Dark Forest and giving in to panic instead of helping their descendants and persuades them to unify and fight side by side with the Lake Clans. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Dovewing</b> also fulfils her part of the prophecy when she <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[uses her powers to listen what is happening in the Dark Forest and manages to warn the Clans about the time of attack <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <b>Lionblaze</b>, on the other hand… I really love Lionblaze, and he is my favourite character in ‘Omen of the Stars’ arc – a level-headed and mature warrior trying to find his path in life had grown a lot from that hot-headed, not-caring-for-consequences apprentice we’ve seen in ‘The Power of Three’ arc. But I expected Lionblaze's part in the final battle to be more spectacular, like the epic fights he had in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6547563.Fading_Echoes__Warriors_Omen_of_the_Stars___2_" title="Fading Echoes (Warriors Omen of the Stars, #2) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Fading Echoes</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7217724.Night_Whispers__Warriors_Omen_of_the_Stars__3_" title="Night Whispers (Warriors Omen of the Stars #3) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Night Whispers</a>. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[True, he does fight, but he doesn't seem to be as good in it as in previous books. First, he is beaten up by Shredtail, who is not very high-ranked in the Dark Forest, and then he is defeated by Breezepelt of all cats – and Lionblaze actually needs Crowfeather to save him out of this situation! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>The Fourth Cat</b>, though, is the one who plays one of the most important roles. Once this cat is found, their addition to the prophecy becomes very logical and clear. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The books had started with Firestar as the hero, so it is fitting that they end on the same note. Besides, Firestar is a Clan leader – he is older, wiser and more experienced than the other heroes. His input into the battle with the Dark Forest is not only that he fights, but more than that: it is Firestar who united Clan leaders so that they can fight the Dark Forest as one, it is him who developed the plan to defend their camps. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />What gives the book a massive credit in my eyes is also that <b>side and minor characters</b> are at their best as well – and since it’s the final book, these characters were with me for a long, long time and therefore especially dear to me. Mothwing, for example, is one of my personal favourites. It’s interesting that her lack of faith in StarClan gave her an unusual clarity of mind and ability to think for herself. When others blindly follow StarClan’s dogmas, Mothwing follows the spirit of the law of medicine cats, which tells them to reach across borders and help cats regardless of their Clans. Mothwing truly has determination of the warrior and wisdom of the medicine cat.<br /><br />Dovewing and Tigerheart are one of the sweetest couples in the series, and I while I love Bumblestripe as a character, I prefer Dovewing and Tigerheart. I just wish Tigerheart to go to ThunderClan or Dovewing to go to ShadowClan, doesn’t really matter which of then would change Clans. With so many inter-Clan romances either ending tragically or leaving cats bitter and angry, I want at least one to have a happy ending. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And while there is no clear answer in the book, I still have my hopes… <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />There are choices to be made, and it was so heartwarming that Cinderheart had finally made hers. The poor cat had spent the last two books confused about what life she was supposed to live, whose destiny she was supposed to follow and even who she was. Finally, she had chosen the path she is going to take... and the cat she is going to walk it with. After all the obstacles she and Lionblaze had to overcome, they can finally walk this path together. And it’s so good to see that Brambleclaw, Squirrelflight and Leafpool were finally able to make peace for all of their past deeds and forgive each other. After so much time spent suffering, the heartbreak is over.<br /><br />The battle with the Dark Forest is cruel and vicious, and there are deaths. All deaths are hard, but very often I feel that there is sense and a sort of epicness as well <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[– even if we take Mousefur who was killed by an unnamed cat or Ferncloud dying at the nursery’s entrance. Even though it was quite a time since they hunted and fought for the Clan, they still were warriors, and they died like ones – protecting their Clan. Or Beetlewhisker who had died even before the battle started – but he showed the most glaring miscalculation on the part of the Dark Forest: the real warriors always know where their loyalty lies. Or Hollyleaf. I never knew what to think about Hollyleaf. I loved her as apprentice, but hated her after the events of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/5269697.Sunrise__Warriors_Power_of_Three___6_" title="Sunrise (Warriors Power of Three, #6) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">Sunrise</a>. Her return in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7124925.The_Forgotten_Warrior__Warriors_Omen_of_the_Stars___5_" title="The Forgotten Warrior (Warriors Omen of the Stars, #5) by Erin Hunter" rel="nofollow noopener">The Forgotten Warrior</a> evened things a bit, but I still felt like she didn’t belong with the Clans. Maybe I’ll say a cruel thing, but when she died protecting her Clanmate, it seemed like a very appropriate ending of her story – her path from a loyal warrior to the traitor and to her redemption that earned her a place in the stars <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17260105694399566554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Toni" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/71332652-toni"><img alt="Toni" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2272606633?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Toni" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Toni" href="/user/show/71332652-toni">Toni</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2272606633" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1386139053023287822">i got so excited when spottedleaf came back. i just have to get that out of the way. <br/>with that said, this book was an interesting and semi satisfying read. the atmosphere was moderately calm, up until the end of the book. the read is worth it.<br/>though poor jayfeather is accused of murdering flametail (in an earlier book), he’s still able to talk to mothwing, which is good. gladly, after searching for flametail’s spirit, jay’s able to convince him that he wasn’t murdered and that was a pretty satis</span>
  <span id="freeText1386139053023287822" style="display:none">i got so excited when spottedleaf came back. i just have to get that out of the way. <br />with that said, this book was an interesting and semi satisfying read. the atmosphere was moderately calm, up until the end of the book. the read is worth it.<br />though poor jayfeather is accused of murdering flametail (in an earlier book), he’s still able to talk to mothwing, which is good. gladly, after searching for flametail’s spirit, jay’s able to convince him that he wasn’t murdered and that was a pretty satisfying moment. what wasn’t satisfying, though, was the reveal that there was a 4th cat in the prophecy. the three were fine as they were, and a 4th cat just made it convoluted and more confusing than it needed to be. <br />the battle redeemed the satisfaction in my eyes, as a bunch of cats whom i was sad that passed care back, but only for a little bit. i was most excited when spottedleaf re-appeared, but when she was killed off for a second time it made me a little more salty than i thought i’d be. <br />firestar’s death was a breath of fresh air. oh my god how excited i was when he took his last breath. almost everything in that series revolved around that one cat and seeing him go was a great read. <br />overall, i’d recommend this to others. sorry not sorry that i spoiled. </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('f8d2gmU7GQYNHDAtz0qXEG6wqSV6v/IU09x08N6lqsrX+9A70+/Nsfw5zqauuwW2kaGiJ4FhSlmIKVdrawFbJw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6znSR2d4ac7Yql3Q0Emm+WP9DZRBC/IG6Jkud5T+vaFDBXT+0ay9eSmPo1uxuDRfnOwGlrrVSkuzbA3sIVpMTA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText1680829948279150657" style="display:none">Erin Hunter is the pseudonym of five people: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/132369.Kate_Cary" title="Kate Cary" rel="nofollow noopener">Kate Cary</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/220345.Cherith_Baldry" title="Cherith Baldry" rel="nofollow noopener">Cherith Baldry</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/374504.Tui_T__Sutherland" title="Tui T. Sutherland" rel="nofollow noopener">Tui T. Sutherland</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2742182.Gillian_Philip" title="Gillian Philip" rel="nofollow noopener">Gillian Philip</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/769868.Inbali_Iserles" title="Inbali Iserles" rel="nofollow noopener">Inbali Iserles</a>, as well as editor <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/645010.Victoria_Holmes" title="Victoria Holmes" rel="nofollow noopener">Victoria Holmes</a>. Together, they write the Warriors series as well as the Seekers and Survivors series. Erin Hunter is working on a new series now called Bravelands. <br /><br />Erin Hunter is inspired by a love of cats and a fascination with the ferocity of the natural world. As well as having a great respect for nature in all its forms, Erin enjoys creating rich mythical explanations for animal behavior, shaped by her interest in astronomy and standing stones.</span>

      <div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/work/quotes/7386615-the-last-hope-warriors-omen-of-the-stars-6">Quotes from The Last Hope</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;There will be three cats, kin of your kin, with the power of the stars in their paws. They will find a fourth, and the battle between light and dark will be won. A new leader will rise from the shadows of his death, and the clan will survive beyond thge memories of his memeries. This is how it has always been and alway will be.&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/535041-there-will-be-three-cats-kin-of-your-kin-with">53 likes</a>
            </nobr>
            <div class="clear"></div>
          </div>
          <div class="stacked" tyle="padding-bottom:15px">
            <span class="readable">&ldquo;My head is so full of memories!" Cinderheart wailed. "I feel as though there are two lives inside me, not one. How can it be my choice to make? Doesn't Cinderpelt have a choice? I can't make her a warrior! She was a medicine cat!"<br />Lionblaze pressed his muzzle closer. "She chose you", he murmured. "She gave you the choice".<br />Cinderheart began to tremble. Lionblaze could sense her mind whirling. "You can only live one life, Cinderheart. It's your choice! This is your destiny, not Cinderpelt's. She lived her own life".<br />Cinderheart gasped. Then her pelt smoothed. She lifted her chin. "Then I choose the life of a warrior". Her blue eyes shone. "And I choose you".<br />A breeze stirred the ferns. Lionblaze glimpsed a pale gray shape appear like a shadow beside Cinderheart. Stepping back in surprise, he saw it peel away from her and drift up like a cobweb carried by the wind. A soft voice whispered, Thank you. <br />Lionblaze's fur stood on end. "Did you see that?<br />Cinderheart was watching the shadow disappear into the trees. "It was Cinderpelt", she breathed. "I've set her free".<br />Lionblaze purred loudly. "Will you fight alongside me?"<br />Cinderheart pressed her muzzle fiercely against his. "Always".&rdquo;</span>
            <nobr>
              &mdash;
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/quotes/535341-my-head-is-so-full-of-memories-cinderheart-wailed-i">52 likes</a>
            </nobr>
